<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Customer and</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Business
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Relationships</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Business Conduct</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">The&nbsp;way&nbsp;we&nbsp;do&nbsp;business</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">worldwide</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">January 2008</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
 9
</FONT></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="29%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="69%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top" ROWSPAN="3"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What can I do if a reseller complains to me about low prices at another reseller?</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Advise the reseller that you can&#146;t discuss or attempt to influence pricing of other parties, since this could violate antitrust laws.</FONT></P></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ROWSPAN="8"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Competition and Trade Practices</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Laws regulating competition and trade practices vary around the world, but certain activities, such as price fixing and
agreeing with a competitor to allocate customers, are almost always illegal.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">You should not:</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Agree with competitors or exchange information with competitors on prices, policies, contract terms, costs, inventories, marketing plans, or capacity
plans.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Agree with a competitor that the competitor will sell goods and services to Customer A (and you will not), and that you will sell goods and services to Customer B (and your competitor
will not).</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Agree with resellers on the resale pricing of Apple products without Legal Department approval.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Require vendors to purchase
Apple products in order to sell products or services to Apple.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Describe the products or services of competitors inaccurately to promote Apple products or services.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Engage in any pricing or other practices that could defraud a supplier or others.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Violate fair bidding practices, including bidding quiet
periods.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Endorsements</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">When representing Apple, never endorse a product or service of another
business or an individual, unless the endorsement has been approved by your manager. This does not apply to products of other businesses that are sold by Apple.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Open Source Software</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Open source software is software that is available free or at a very low cost. Before using any open source software on Apple equipment or as part of an
Apple software development effort, review the open source software guidelines and contact the Legal Department for approval.</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top" ROWSPAN="5"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What is an example of an endorsement?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A friend writes a great book on software design and asks you to endorse the book by making a statement on the back cover. If you make such an endorsement, don&#146;t include your job title or affiliation with Apple.
</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="1%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="25%"></TD>

<TD></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Governments and</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Communities</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Business Conduct</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">The&nbsp;way&nbsp;we&nbsp;do&nbsp;business</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">worldwide</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">January 2008</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">10</FONT></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="29%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="69%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top" ROWSPAN="8"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Tell me more about pricing products that are sold to U.S. and non-U.S. governments. Governments shouldn&#146;t be charged
more for our products or services than Apple charges other customers for the same products or services. There are laws that make it a crime to overcharge the U.S. government. Some other countries have similar laws.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Can I avoid a gift limitation by paying for a gift, such as lunch or
golf, myself?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">No. If you are representing Apple, any gift to a government employee would be viewed as coming from Apple.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What is considered a gift to a U.S. or foreign official?</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In most cases, anything of value that is given is considered a gift. This includes items such as meals, golf, entertainment, and product samples. Cash is
never an acceptable gift. Typically, giving cash is viewed as a bribe or kickback and is against Apple policy.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What is the difference between a facilitating payment and an illegal payment?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A
facilitating payment is anything of value given to a foreign official for the purpose of expediting performance of certain routine, nondiscretionary activities. An illegal payment is anything of value given to a foreign official for the purpose of
obtaining or retaining business or to secure an improper advantage.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Who is considered a foreign official?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For purposes of the Foreign Corrupt Practices Act, a &#147;foreign official&#148; is any
official or employee of a foreign government, a public international organization (such as the European Commission), any department or agency thereof, or any person acting in an official capacity. This could also include an official of a wholly or
substantially state-owned business enterprise, such as a state-owned public utility.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ROWSPAN="8"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Governments as Customers</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Governments are unique customers for Apple. Governments often place special bidding, pricing, disclosure, and certification requirements on firms with
which they do business. Discuss these requirements with the appropriate Apple attorney before bidding for government business. For example, Apple may have to certify that it is supplying the government with the lowest price charged to Apple&#146;s
commercial customers. Apple may also have to certify that its prices have been arrived at independently&#151;that is, without collaboration with a third party.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gifts&#151;even small items such as a meal or T-shirt&#151;may be prohibited when dealing with government officials. In
addition, there may be special reporting requirements related to gifts. (See the sections that follow for more information on gifts.)</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gifts to U.S. Officials</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">It may be illegal to give a gift, even an inexpensive meal or a T-shirt, to a government employee. The rules vary depending on the location of the
employee (for example, rules may vary by state, school district, and city) and the position held by the employee (for example, there may be different rules for various elected and nonelected officials). If you work with government officials, check
with Government Affairs to determine whether gifting is permitted and the legal limitations on gifts.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To prevent violations, review planned gifts to government officials with Government Affairs in advance of giving a gift.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Gifts to Non-U.S. Officials</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In many countries it is considered common courtesy to provide token gifts on certain occasions to government officials to help build relationships. Check
local requirements and review any such gifts exceeding US$25 in advance with the Legal Department.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Offering or giving anything of value to a foreign official for the purpose of obtaining or retaining business or to secure any improper advantage is illegal. There is a very limited exception for
&#147;facilitating payments &#148; to foreign officials to expedite performance of routine activities such as obtaining permits or licenses; processing visas and work permits; or providing police, mail, or inspection services. All facilitating
payments must be preauthorized by the Legal Department and properly recorded and accounted for. Check with your manager or finance representative to determine the appropriate manner of reporting them.</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="69%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What if I&#146;d like to explore hiring a current government employee as a consultant?</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Contact the Legal Department before beginning any negotiations.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ROWSPAN="5"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Hiring Government Employees</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">U.S. laws limit the duties and types of services that former U.S. government and military employees may perform as employees or consultants of Apple.
In the U.S., employment negotiations with government employees are prohibited while the employees are participating in a matter involving Apple&#146;s interests.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Trade Restrictions and Export Controls</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Many countries periodically impose restrictions on exports and other dealings with certain other countries, persons, or groups.
Export laws may control trading of commodities or technologies that are considered to be strategically important because they have the potential to be used for military purposes. Laws may cover travel to or from a sanctioned country, imports or
exports, new investments, and other related topics. Certain laws also prohibit support of boycott activities. See Apple&#146;s Export Control policy for more information.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If your work involves the sale or shipment of products, technologies, or services across international borders, check with the
Export Department to ensure compliance with any laws or restrictions that apply.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Environment, Health, and Safety</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Apple operates in a manner that conserves the environment and protects the safety and health of our employees. Conduct your job safely and consistent with applicable environmental, health, and safety requirements. Use good judgment and
always put the environment, safety, and health first. Be proactive in anticipating and dealing with environmental, health, and safety risks.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Community Activities</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At Apple, we comply with all laws and regulations and operate in ways that benefit the communities in which we conduct business. Apple encourages you to
uphold this commitment to the community in all your activities.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">If you hold an elected or appointed public office while employed at Apple, advise Government Affairs. Excuse yourself from involvement in any decisions that might create or appear to create a conflict of interest.</FONT></P></TD></TR>

STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Visit the Environment+Safety site.</FONT></P></TD>

<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What are assets?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Assets
include Apple&#146;s extremely valuable proprietary information (such as intellectual property, confidential business plans, unannounced product plans, sales and marketing strategies, and other trade secrets); as well as physical assets like cash,
equipment, supplies, and product inventory.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Where can I
learn more about information protection and nondisclosure agreements?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">View the Apple policy on Confidential, Proprietary, and Trade Secret
Information.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If I believe that it is appropriate to
disclose confidential proprietary information to a vendor or other third party, what should I do?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">First, verify that there is a business
need for the disclosure. Second, obtain your manager&#146;s approval for the disclosure. Third, be sure that a nondisclosure agreement is in place with the vendor or third party, and that you forward the original copy of the agreement to the Legal
Department. If you are still unsure, check with the Legal Department before making the disclosure.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">How do I identify confidential Apple information in documents?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Mark these documents &#147;Apple Confidential.&#148;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What if I have a specific question on the use of the Apple name, names of products or services, or the Apple logo?</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Please direct questions about the Apple corporate identity to corpID@apple.com.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Protecting Apple&#146;s Assets and Information</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Protect Apple&#146;s assets:</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As an Apple employee you have a personal responsibility to
protect Apple&#146;s property. You should follow all security procedures, and be on the lookout for any instances you believe could lead to loss, misuse, or theft of company property. You should protect physical assets such as equipment, supplies,
cash, and charge cards. And you should use extreme care to protect from disclosure to any third parties Apple&#146;s proprietary information, including without limitation technical product information, information related to current and future
products and services, confidential market research, sales and marketing plans, nonpublic earnings or financial data, and organizational charts and information.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Follow procurement policies and
procedures when acquiring goods or services on behalf of Apple, avoiding any real or apparent conflict of interest. For more information on procurement policies and procedures, talk to your manager or visit Apple Procurement.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Use Apple&#146;s assets in a manner that prevents damage, waste, misuse, or theft. Use assets only for legal and ethical purposes.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Dispose of assets only with appropriate approval and in compliance with applicable policies. Before disposing of assets, discuss your plans with your manager.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Confidential Apple Information</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">One of Apple&#146;s greatest assets is information about our products
and services, including future product offerings. Never disclose confidential operational, financial, trade secret, or other business information without verifying with your manager that such disclosure is appropriate. Typically, disclosure of this
information is very limited, and the information may be shared with vendors, suppliers, or other third parties only after a nondisclosure agreement is in place. Even within Apple, confidential information should be shared only on a need-to-know
basis. The Intellectual Property Agreement you signed when you joined Apple defines your duty to protect information.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Apple Identity and Trademarks</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Apple name, names of products (such as iPod), names of services (such as AppleCare), tag lines (such as &#147;Don&#146;t steal music&#148;), and logos
(such as the familiar Apple logo) collectively create the Apple identity. Before publicly using the Apple name, product names, service names, tag lines, or the Apple logo, visit the Marketing site and select &#147;Corporate Identity&#148; for
specific guidelines. Before using</FONT></P></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:120px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:24px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">How can I learn more about procedures for meals and travel?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">See Apple&#146;s Travel policy or talk to your manager.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:24px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:24px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:24px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="font-size:24px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:24px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If I suspect money laundering, what should I do?</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Advise your manager or contact the Apple Legal Department.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Copyright Protection</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you create original material for Apple that requires copyright protection, such as software, place Apple&#146;s copyright notice on the work and submit
a copyright disclosure form to the Legal Department. For more information, visit the Apple Copyright Information site.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Accuracy of Records and Reports</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Accurate records are critical to meeting Apple&#146;s legal, financial, and management obligations. Ensure that all records and reports, including
customer information, technical and product information, correspondence, and public communications, are full, fair, accurate, timely, and understandable.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Never misstate facts, omit critical information, or modify records or reports in any way to mislead others, or assist others in doing so.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Business Expenses</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All employees must observe policies and procedures regarding business
expenses, such as meal and travel expenses, and submit accurate expense reimbursement requests. Guidelines on daily meal expenses vary worldwide.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Establishing Bank Accounts</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All Apple bank accounts must be approved and established by Apple&#146;s Treasury Department. All payments must be made by recordable and traceable
methods. For more information, contact the Treasury Department.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Loans, Advances, and Guarantees</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Other than
through established corporate programs, such as programs for employee relocation and the cashless exercise of stock options, Apple does not provide loans or advances of corporate funds to its employees, officers, Board members, or their families and
does not guarantee their obligations.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Money Laundering
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Money laundering is the process by which individuals or
organizations try to conceal illicit funds or make these funds look legitimate. If you are in a position to deal directly with customers or vendors, the following examples may be indications of potential money laundering:</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Attempts to make large payments in cash</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Payments by someone who is not a party to the
contract</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Requests to pay more than provided for in the contract</FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Tell me more about &#147;legal holds.&#148;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In a litigation case or other legal matter, Apple may be required to produce documents. In these cases the Legal Department may put a &#147;legal hold&#148; on certain documents to prevent the documents from being
destroyed, altered, or modified. If it is found that Apple has failed to retain or produce required documents, penalties or adverse rulings may result. Adverse rulings in major litigation cases can cost Apple a significant amount of money. Failure
of employees to retain and preserve documents placed on a legal hold may result in discipline or discharge.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Document Retention and Legal Hold</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As an Apple employee, you have a responsibility to manage documents and make decisions on document retention. The definition of &#147;document&#148; is
extremely broad. For example, every email or other electronic file, every customer record, and every transaction involves the creation of a document. Different documents have different retention periods. Check with your manager or contact Records
Management to determine the appropriate retention period for documents in your area.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At times, Apple may need to retain documents beyond the period they would normally be retained. The most common reasons are litigation or other legal matters. In these situations, retention and preservation of
documents is critical. If you have documents that may be required for litigation or other legal matters, the Legal Department will place those documents on a &#147;legal hold,&#148; meaning the documents cannot be altered, destroyed, deleted, or
modified in any manner, and will inform the individuals most closely identified with the documents. Instructions for retaining the documents will be provided, and you must ensure that these instructions are followed. A legal hold remains in effect
until you are notified by the Legal Department in writing.</FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Can you give an example of conflicts of interest or potential divided loyalty?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Your brother-in-law owns a business, that business is being considered as a vendor for Apple, and you are one of the decision makers.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">May I occasionally use my Apple email address for my outside business?
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Limited personal use of your Apple email is permitted for activities such as sending a brief message to a friend. You may never use your
Apple email for an outside business.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">I&#146;m working on
an invention on my own time. Does Apple need to know?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If your invention relates to your job at Apple or could compete with current or
reasonably anticipated future products or services of Apple, disclose the invention to your manager.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">May I serve on the board of directors of an outside enterprise or organization?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you
plan to serve on a board, you must obtain approval from your manager and the Senior Vice President for your organization. In addition, Vice Presidents and Executive Team members must obtain the approval of their manager and the CEO before they can
accept a position on the board of directors of a private or publicly traded company (other than nonprofit entities).</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What does &#147;significant personal relationship&#148; mean?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Significant personal relationships include close friends and relatives and may even include a long-term acquaintance or neighbor. If you are unsure, the best approach is to disclose the potential conflict to your
manager.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Conflicts of Interest</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A conflict of interest is any activity that is inconsistent with or opposed to Apple&#146;s best interests, or that gives the appearance of impropriety or
divided loyalty. Avoid any situation that creates a real or perceived conflict of interest. Use good judgment, and if you are unsure about a potential conflict, talk to your manager, contact Human Resources, check with the Legal Department, or
contact the Business Conduct Helpline.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Outside Employment
and Inventions</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you are a full-time Apple employee,
taking any other employment, full-time or part-time, requires that you notify your manager. In addition, any employee (full-time or part-time) who obtains outside employment (such as a part-time job away from Apple), has an outside business, or is
working on an invention must comply with the following rules.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Do not:</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Use any time at work or any Apple assets for your other job, outside business, or invention. This includes using Apple workspace, telephones, computers, Internet access, copy machines,
and any other Apple assets or services.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Use your position at Apple to solicit work for your outside business or other employer, to obtain favored treatment, or to pressure others to assist you in working
on your invention.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Use confidential Apple information to benefit your other employer, outside business, or invention.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Participate in an outside
employment activity that could have an adverse effect on your ability to perform your duties at Apple.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2.00em; text-indent:-2.00em" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Participate in an outside business or outside employment,
or develop an invention, that is in an area of Apple&#146;s present or reasonably anticipated future business. Before participating in inventions or businesses that are in the same area as your work for Apple or that compete with Apple products or
services, you must have written permission from your manager, an Apple product law attorney, and the Executive Team member in your organization.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Significant Personal Relationships</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Do not conduct Apple business with family members or others with whom you have a significant personal relationship. In rare cases where exceptions may be
appropriate, written approval from the Senior Vice President for your organization is required.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">You shouldn&#146;t use your position at Apple to obtain favored treatment for yourself, family members, or others with whom</FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="1%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="23%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="1%"></TD>
<TD></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Individual</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Conduct</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Business Conduct</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">The&nbsp;way&nbsp;we&nbsp;do&nbsp;business</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">worldwide</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">January 2008</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">20</FONT></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="29%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="69%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">I have stock in companies that do business with Apple. Is this a problem?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">It&#146;s unlikely that this is a problem. However, it could be a concern if (1)&nbsp;you&#146;re influencing a transaction between Apple and the company, and (2)&nbsp;the transaction is
significant enough to potentially affect the value of your investment.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">How do I know whether information is material?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Determining what constitutes material information is a matter
of judgment. In general, information is material if it would likely be considered important by an investor purchasing or selling Apple securities or securities of other companies.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Does Apple&#146;s policy apply to buying or selling stock in other companies?</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Yes. For example, say you learn about a customer&#146;s nonpublic expansion plans through discussions about hardware purchases. If you purchase stock in
the customer&#146;s company or advise others to do so, it could be viewed as insider trading.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What is harassment?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Harassment is unwelcome or unsolicited speech or conduct based on
factors such as race, color, age, sex, or sexual orientation. It may include activities such as viewing sexually explicit sites or displaying an inappropriate calendar. It may include unwelcome touching or advances, jokes, slurs, and other offensive
behavior.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Personal Investments</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Many Apple employees have investments in publicly traded stock or privately held businesses. If you hold shares of a publicly traded business or have any
ownership in a privately held business, a conflict may exist if you are involved in or attempt to influence transactions between Apple and the business in which you are invested.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If a real or apparent conflict exists, disclose the conflict to your manager. The manager will help determine whether a
conflict exists and, if appropriate, the best approach to eliminate the conflict.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Buying and Selling Stock</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Never buy or sell stock while you are in possession of information obtained through your employment at Apple if the information has not been publicly announced and could have a material effect on the value of the investment. This applies to
decisions to buy or sell Apple securities and to investments in other companies. It is also against Apple policy and may be illegal under U.S. law to give others, such as friends and family members, tips on when to buy or sell stock while you are in
possession of material, nonpublic information concerning that stock. In addition, employees are prohibited from investing in derivatives of Apple&#146;s securities. This includes, but is not limited to, trading in put or call options related to
securities of the company.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Members of Apple&#146;s Board
of Directors, executive officers, and certain other individuals are subject to blackout periods during which they are prohibited from trading in Apple stock. If you are subject to these restrictions, you&#146;ll be notified by the Legal Department.
However, as a reminder, you may never buy or sell stock while you are in possession of material, nonpublic information regardless of being subject to blackout periods.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review Apple&#146;s Insider Trading policy and summary of trading blackout dates. Specific questions on buying and selling
stock should be referred to the Legal Department.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Harassment and Discrimination</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Apple encourages a
creative, culturally diverse, and supportive work environment. Apple does not tolerate harassment or discrimination based on factors such as race, color, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity characteristics or expression, religion, national
origin, age, marital status, disability, medical condition, veteran status, or pregnancy. Additional restrictions may apply based on regional laws and regulations.</FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Where can I learn more about policies on confidential employee information?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">View the Apple Safe Harbor Privacy Policy.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Is personal information on my computer system private?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Limited personal use of Apple
equipment and systems is allowed, but subject to local regulations, Apple may monitor equipment and systems. If in doubt, check with the Legal Department.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">What if I have a substance abuse issue?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Help yourself and Apple by taking action. Talk to your Human Resources representative or, in the U.S., view information on the Employee Assistance Program.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">How do I reach Corporate Communications?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In the U.S., call 408-974-2042. Outside the U.S., check with your manager.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If I make a presentation on my own time, may I accept a payment?</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">That depends. If you
are representing Apple, you may not accept payment. If you are on your own time and are not representing Apple, you may be allowed to accept payment. Before accepting this type of opportunity, check with your manager, Human Resources, or the
Business Conduct Helpline.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Confidential Employee Information</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As part of your job, you may have access to information regarding other Apple employees or applicants. This may range from employment history to personal
contact information to health information to information on investment decisions. Such information is confidential and should be shared only with those who have a business need to know the information. It also should not be shared outside Apple
unless there is a legal or business reason to share the information and your manager approves.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Privacy</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Subject to rules or regulations affecting an employee&#146;s rights, Apple may monitor or search its work environments, including equipment, networks, mail, and electronic systems, without notice. Apple monitors facilities and equipment to
promote safety, prevent unlawful activity, investigate misconduct, manage information systems, comply with legal guidelines, and for other business purposes.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Substance Use or Abuse</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Use of alcohol or other drugs on the job or before work can cause safety issues, damage customer relations, and hurt productivity and innovation. Use good
judgment and keep in mind that you are expected to perform to your full ability when working for Apple.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Public Communications</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All public communications, speaking opportunities, and inquiries from the press or the financial analyst community must be referred to Corporate Communications or the Investor Relations Department.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Honoraria and Public Speaking</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All public speaking engagements in which you represent Apple must be
preapproved by your manager and Corporate Communications. If you receive approval to make a public presentation at a business meeting or conference, you may not request or accept any form of personal compensation from the organization that requested
the presentation. This does not prohibit accepting reimbursement for expenses, if approved by your manager.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Publishing Articles</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you author an article or other publication, do not identify yourself in the publication as an employee of Apple without prior approval from Corporate Communications. This could be viewed as an endorsement by Apple.
</FONT></P></TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Taking Action</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Business Conduct</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">The&nbsp;way&nbsp;we&nbsp;do&nbsp;business</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">worldwide</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="29%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="69%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Your Obligation to Take Action</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Always apply Apple&#146;s principles of business conduct, follow Apple policies, and comply with laws and regulations. When you are unsure, take the
initiative to investigate the right course of action. Check with your manager, Human Resources, Legal, Internal Audit, or Finance, or review our policies on AppleWeb. If you would like to talk with someone outside your immediate area, consider
contacting the Business Conduct Helpline.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you have
knowledge of possible violations of Apple&#146;s business conduct principles, policies, or legal and regulatory requirements, you must notify your manager, Human Resources, Legal, Internal Audit, Finance, or the Business Conduct Helpline.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Business Conduct Helpline</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Business Conduct Helpline is available to all employees worldwide
and is active 24/7. It helps to answer your questions on business conduct issues, policies, regulations, and compliance with legal requirements and Apple&#146;s business conduct policy. It also allows you to advise Apple of situations that may
require investigation or management attention.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The
Business Conduct Helpline is committed to keeping your issues and identity confidential. If you would be more comfortable doing so, you may contact the Helpline anonymously. Your information will be shared only with those who have a need to know,
such as those involved in answering your questions or investigating and correcting issues you raise. Note that if your information involves accounting, finance, or auditing, the law requires that necessary information be shared with the Audit and
Finance Committee of Apple&#146;s Board of Directors.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In
France, due to legal restrictions, anonymous use of the Business Conduct Helpline is discouraged and the Helpline may be used only to report accounting, finance, and auditing issues.</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">When you use the Business Conduct Helpline to report an issue, you are
protected from any form of retaliation. Retaliation will not be tolerated.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" align="left">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Business Conduct Helpline is available on AppleWeb. Access the Business Conduct Helpline.</FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<FILENAME>dex311.htm
<DESCRIPTION>RULE 13A-14(A) / 15D-14(A) CERTIFICATION OF CHIEF EXECUTIVE OFFICER
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Rule 13a-14(a) / 15d-14(a) Certification of Chief Executive Officer</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 31.1 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>CERTIFICATIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">I, Steven P. Jobs, certify that: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">I have reviewed this quarterly report on Form 10-Q of Apple Inc.; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Based on my knowledge, this report does not contain any untrue statement of a material fact or omit to state a material fact necessary to make the statements
made, in light of the circumstances under which such statements were made, not misleading with respect to the period covered by this report; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">3.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Based on my knowledge, the financial statements, and other financial information included in this report, fairly present in all material respects the financial
condition, results of operations and cash flows of the registrant as of, and for, the periods presented in this report; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">4.</FONT></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The registrant&#146;s other certifying officer(s) and I are responsible for establishing and maintaining disclosure controls and procedures (as defined in
Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e)) and internal control over financial reporting (as defined in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(f) and 15d-15(f)) for the registrant and have: </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a)</FONT></P></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Designed such disclosure controls and procedures, or caused such disclosure controls and procedures to be designed under our supervision, to ensure that material
information relating to the registrant, including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to us by others within those entities, particularly during the period in which this report is being prepared; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
